## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: classical mechanics (nonlinear oscillations / dynamical systems)
**Analysis**: The target dv_dt is acceleration and the available state variables are x (position) and v (velocity), which matches second-order equations of motion for (nonlinear) oscillators: x' = v, v' = dv_dt = f(x, v, t). Common models combine a restoring force term in x, damping/anti-damping in v, and optional explicit time-dependent forcing/parametric modulation in t.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear (damped) harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (small oscillations with linear restoring force and viscous damping)
- Time-dependent drive (forced oscillator): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t + c4) (external periodic forcing)
- Constant + periodic forcing offset: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (bias plus harmonic excitation)
- Duffing oscillator (cubic stiffness): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (hardening/softening spring nonlinearity with damping)
- Higher-order stiffness nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 + c3 * v (strongly nonlinear restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping (quadratic/cubic drag): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v * Abs(v) (aerodynamic-type damping) 
- Cubic (Rayleigh-type) damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (amplitude-dependent damping, can generate self-excited oscillations with sign choices)
- Van der Pol oscillator (Liénard form): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (c2 - x**2) * v (self-excited oscillator with limit cycle)
- General Liénard oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + (c1 + c2 * x**2 + c3 * x**4) * v (state-dependent damping with nonlinear restoring)
- Parametric stiffness modulation: dv_dt = (c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x + c3 * v (Mathieu/parametrically excited oscillator)
- Nonlinear parametric modulation: dv_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * x + c3 * x**3 + c4 * v (parametric drive plus Duffing nonlinearity)
- Conservative force from a nonlinear potential: dv_dt = -(c0 * x + c1 * x**3) (undamped conservative motion; depends only on x)
- Pendulum small-to-moderate angle model: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) + c2 * v (trigonometric restoring force with damping)
- Mixed coupling term (nonlinear inertia/feedback proxy): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (amplitude-dependent dissipation or feedback)
- Driven nonlinear oscillator with harmonics: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * sin(c4 * t) + c5 * sin(c6 * t) (multi-tone excitation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Purely conservative oscillation (no dissipation/forcing) often yields dv_dt as a function of x only (e.g., odd restoring force), implying approximate energy conservation and closed phase-plane orbits.
- Viscous damping produces a term proportional to v; if its coefficient is negative (i.e., dv_dt contains +|c|*v), it indicates energy injection/instability rather than dissipation.
- Hardening/softening stiffness is suggested by odd nonlinear terms in x (x**3, x**5): positive cubic stiffness tends to harden (frequency increases with amplitude), negative tends to soften.
- Aerodynamic/frictional losses often introduce nonlinear odd-in-v terms like v*Abs(v) or v**3, giving stronger damping at higher speeds and non-exponential amplitude decay.
- Self-excited limit cycles are indicated by state-dependent damping such as (c0 - x**2)*v (negative damping at small |x| and positive damping at large |x|).
- Explicit periodic dependence on t in coefficients multiplying x (e.g., (c0 + c1*cos(c2*t))*x) is characteristic of parametric excitation and can cause instability bands (Mathieu-type behavior).
- External forcing typically appears as additive sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) terms; the presence of multiple harmonics suggests nonlinear response or multi-frequency driving.
- Symmetry: many mechanical oscillators have odd restoring forces (dv_dt changes sign with x), so even powers of x in dv_dt often imply asymmetry, bias, or modeling artifacts (e.g., gravity offset in a shifted coordinate).
- Coupling terms like x**2*v or x*v*Abs(v) can represent amplitude-dependent dissipation/feedback; they often shape phase portraits away from simple ellipses toward distorted limit cycles.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO15)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - omega0**c0*(gamma*Abs(v)**c1 + c2)*x - omega0**c3*x - omega0**c4*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
F(x,t,v)=0.6813255\sin t\;-\;1.8579933\,x\,(0.03553985|v|^{1/3}+1)\;-\;1.8579933\,x\;-\;1.8579933\,x e^{-|x|}
\]
So GT has these essential structural features:

- A pure time sinusoid term: \(A\sin t\) (no \(x\) multiplier).
- A damping-like term proportional to \(x|v|^{1/3}\) (note: **fractional power of \(|v|\)** and multiplied by \(x\)).
- Linear-in-\(x\) terms (two separate contributions, but can be combined into one coefficient times \(x\)).
- A non-polynomial term \(-K\,x e^{-|x|}\) (note: depends on \(|x|\) inside an exponential; **not** \(e^{c t}\), not \(e^{\sin(\cdot)}\), etc.).
- No constant offset term.

Now check each candidate for whether its form can be tuned (via its free constants) to exactly equal the GT for all real \(x,t,v\).

---

### 1.
Has \(c3\exp(c4\sin(c5+c6 t))\) and \(c7\sin(c8 x+c9)\). GT needs \(x e^{-|x|}\) (exponential in \(|x|\), multiplied by \(x\)), and \(\sin(t)\) (not \(\exp(\sin)\), and not \(\sin\) of \(x\)). Cannot create \(x e^{-|x|}\) or \(x|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 2.
Contains \(\sin(c3+c4 t)/(c5+x^2)^{1/3}\), polynomial \(x^3,x^5\), and \(x\cos(c9 t)\). GT needs \(x e^{-|x|}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\) at all; no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 3.
Has \(c1|x|\) and \(\sin(\cdot)/(c6+x^2)^{1/3}\), plus polynomials. Still no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\) term. Also \(|x|\) cannot mimic \(x e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 4.
Same issue as 2/3: no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 5.
Only trig in \(t\) (sin/cos) and polynomials in \(x\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 6.
Has \(\exp(c4\sin(c5 t+c6 x+c7))\): exponential of sine, not \(e^{-|x|}\), and not multiplied by \(x\) in the required way. No \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 7.
Has \(v^2\), \(x^2\), and \((c5+x^2)^2\sin(\cdot)\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 8.
Same: \((c3+x^2)^2\sin(\cdot)\), polynomials. No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 9.
Has linear \(v\), cosines in \(t\), and odd powers of \(x\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\), no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 10.
Has \(v\) and \(v^3\), cosines in \(t\), and \(x(c7+x^2)^{1/3}\). GT needs \(x e^{-|x|}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\). Here the fractional power is of \(x\)-expression, not \(|v|\). Also no \(|x|\) in an exponential. **No.**

### 11.
Has \(x^{c7}\) but no exponential-in-\(|x|\), and \(v, v^3\) not \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 12.
Has \(v\,|v|\) (i.e., \(|v|v\)) and \(x(c7+x^2)^{1/3}\). Still cannot produce \(x|v|^{1/3}\) (wrong power and wrong dependence) nor \(x e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 13.
Has \(v\exp(c9 t)\) and polynomials. No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 14.
Same structural mismatch as 10: fractional power in \(x\), not \(|v|\); no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 15.
Same as 14. **No.**

### 16.
Has \(x^{c7}\), \(v\), and \(x\cos(\cdot)\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 17.
Polynomials + \(v\) + cosines. No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 18.
Same as 16. **No.**

### 19.
Has \(v\), \(v x^2\), \(x\cos(\cdot)\), and \(x(c9+x^2)^{1/3}\). No \(e^{-|x|}\). Also \(v\) not \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 20.
Like 10/14 but without higher \(v\) powers. Still no \(e^{-|x|}\) and no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 21.
Has \(x/(c9+x^2)^{3/2}\) (a rational decay), not \(x e^{-|x|}\). Also \(v\) and \(v x^2\) not \(x|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 22.
Adds \(v x^2\) but still no \(|v|^{1/3}\), no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 23.
Has \(v|v|\) (power 2 with sign), not \(|v|^{1/3}\); no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 24.
Has \(v^3\), not \(|v|^{1/3}\); no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 25.
Has \(x\sin(c8 t+c9)\) (time sinusoid multiplied by \(x\)), but GT’s \(\sin t\) term is **not** multiplied by \(x\). Also no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 26.
Has \(v e^{c7 t}\), not \(x e^{-|x|}\), and no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 27.
Has \(v|v|\) and \(v^3\), not \(|v|^{1/3}\); no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 28.
Has \(x/(c3+|x|)^3\) and \(v^{c5} x/(c6+x)\) plus \(v\) and \(\cos(c8 t)\).
- Could set \(c5=1/3\) to get \(v^{1/3}\), but it is **not** \(|v|^{1/3}\); for negative \(v\), \(v^{1/3}\) (real cube root) differs from \(|v|^{1/3}\). GT explicitly uses \(|v|^{1/3}\), and domain includes negative \(v\), so not equivalent.
- Also no \(x e^{-|x|}\); \(x/(c3+|x|)^3\) cannot equal \(x e^{-|x|}\) for all \(x\).
- \(\cos(c8 t)\) could phase-shift to \(\sin t\), but other mismatches remain. **No.**

### 29.
Has \(x/(|x|^3+1)\) and polynomial terms; includes \(v^3\) and \(v x^2\). No \(x e^{-|x|}\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 30.
Has \(x e^{c8 t}\) (exponential in time), not \(x e^{-|x|}\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 31.
Has \(v|x|\) and \(x/(|x|^3+1)\); no \(x e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 32.
Has \(v|v|\) and \(x/(|x|^3+1)\); no \(x e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 33.
Same: no \(x e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 34.
Same: no \(x e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\. **No.**

### 35.
Polynomials + \(v^3\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 36.
Polynomials + \(v|v|\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 37.
Has \((c4+x^2)^2\sin(c5 t+c6)\) and \(x\cos(c9 t)\). GT needs a standalone \(\sin t\) (possible via setting the prefactor independent of \(x\), but here it is multiplied by \((c4+x^2)^2\), which cannot be constant for all \(x\) unless coefficient is 0). Also no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 38.
Has \(x^{c8}\) and \(v x^2\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 39.
Same: no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 40.
Has \(\sin(c7 x+c8)\) (sin of \(x\)), not \(x e^{-|x|}\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 41.
Same as 40 plus \(v x^2\). Still no. **No.**

### 42.
Same as 41 plus \(v x^4\). Still no. **No.**

### 43.
Pure polynomial in \(x\). No \(\sin t\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\), no \(e^{-|x|}\). **No.**

### 44.
Has \(v\log(c9|x|+1)\) but GT needs \(x e^{-|x|}\). Log cannot match exponential for all \(x\). No \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 45.
Polynomials + \(v\) + \(\cos(\cdot)\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 46.
Adds \(v x^2\). Still no \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 47.
Linear \(v\) terms, cos in \(t\), polynomials. No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 48.
Has \(v\log(c9 x^2+1)\) and \(v^3\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 49.
Has \(v, v x^2, v^3\), cos in \(t\), polynomials. No \(e^{-|x|}\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 50.
Has \(v|v|\) and \(v\sin(c7 x+c8)\). No \(e^{-|x|}\), and \(v|v|\neq |v|^{1/3}\). Also \(\sin\) depends on \(x\), not \(t\) for the needed forcing term. **No.**

---

None of the candidates contain (or can be tuned to produce) the crucial GT structures \(x e^{-|x|}\) and \(x|v|^{1/3}\) simultaneously, and several also lack a standalone \(\sin t\) term (or only have \(\cos\) which could be phase-shifted, but other mismatches remain). Therefore no candidate can be made exactly equivalent to the fixed GT over the full sign-changing domain.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (PO15)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - omega0**c0*(gamma*Abs(v)**c1 + c2)*x - omega0**c3*x - omega0**c4*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT numerical expression:**
`-1.85799332865866*x*(0.0355398482733264*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 1.85799332865866*x - 1.85799332865866*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.681325524225947*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
`-1.85799332865866*0.0355398482733264*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) - 1.85799332865866*x - 1.85799332865866*x - 1.85799332865866*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.681325524225947*sin(t)`

= `-0.06601...*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) - 3.71598...*x - 1.85799...*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.681325...*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `x` (linear in x)
2. `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` (coupling of x and fractional power of |v|)
3. `x*exp(-Abs(x))` (x times exponential of -|x|)
4. `sin(t)` (sinusoidal in t)

This is a very specific combination. Let me check each candidate for the presence of these exact basis functions.

**Key requirements:**
- Must have `sin(t)` or equivalent (like `cos(t + phase)`)
- Must have `x*exp(-Abs(x))` or something that can exactly reproduce it
- Must have `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` term
- Must have linear `x` term
- No constant offset (c1=0 possible)

The critical challenge is the `x*exp(-Abs(x))` term. No polynomial in x (x³, x⁵, x⁷...) can exactly reproduce `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. Similarly, `sin(cx)`, `x/(1+|x|³)`, `x*(c+x²)^(1/3)`, `x^c` cannot exactly equal `x*exp(-Abs(x))`.

Also, the `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)` term requires a specific coupling between x and a fractional power of |v|. Terms like `v`, `v³`, `v*|v|`, `v*x²` cannot reproduce this.

Let me quickly scan all candidates:

- **Candidates 1-8**: No `v` dependence matching `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)`, or wrong structure. None have `x*exp(-|x|)`.
- **Candidates 9-50**: Many have `v` terms but as `v`, `v³`, `v*|v|`, `v*x²`, etc. None have `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)`.
- The `x*exp(-|x|)` term is not present in any candidate. Polynomial approximations (x³, x⁵, x⁷) are linearly independent from `x*exp(-|x|)`.
- Candidate 28 has `v**c5*x/(c6+x)` which could give `v^(1/3)*x` behavior but not exactly `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)` since it uses `v` not `Abs(v)`, and the `x/(c6+x)` part cannot equal `x` for all x. Also lacks `x*exp(-|x|)`.
- Candidate 39 has `x**c8` which could be tuned but can't match `x*exp(-|x|)`.

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates contain both the `x*exp(-Abs(x))` basis function AND the `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` basis function needed to match the GT exactly.
